definition the surface \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_aee24cedf48f90a0354c326c1bbcab0a6}{gradient}} is tangent to the surface and has no normal component The surface divergence of an material derivative Rather than covering the here we shall simply$<$ em $>$ ab the governing equations formulated by Lai \&Tseng as well as Cermelli et been discussed many times in the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ac79d3d8efe3b69d0d73dd502db373caf}{literature}} and the main confusion surrounds how material derivatives are taken Unlike the conventional bulk equations the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} does not occupy every point in the so one cannot simply use the standard form of the material derivative Rather than covering the here we shall simply$<$ em $>$ ab the governing equations formulated by Lai \&Tseng as well as Cermelli et who claim it was established by \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a59f1d5bb1b7bcfa71f4a12c7adb5cb13}{Transport}} Equations Consider a chemical species with \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} concentration \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ad1745fb26f1b55045298edac2ccd2d99}{f}} Gamma \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ad1745fb26f1b55045298edac2ccd2d99}{f}} \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a012a850e4f6231372e95c39aff5d5787}{that}} is only present on the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} It can be transported within the moving \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} by the standard mechanisms of advection and but changes in the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} area can also induce changes in its concentration The \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ac5f0c50a2d71349b887edce57abea84a}{formulation}} of \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} transport equations has been discussed many times in the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ac79d3d8efe3b69d0d73dd502db373caf}{literature}} and the main confusion surrounds how material derivatives are taken Unlike the conventional bulk equations the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} does not occupy every point in the so one cannot simply use the standard form of the material derivative Rather than covering the here we shall simply$<$ em $>$ ab the governing equations formulated by Lai \&Tseng as well as Cermelli et who claim it was established by but \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a012a850e4f6231372e95c39aff5d5787}{that}} it leads to a simpler \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ac5f0c50a2d71349b887edce57abea84a}{formulation}} which avoids calculation of the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a6617e7f8f08558a13bf7d453c350197b}{curvature}} (and hence second derivatives). \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ad1745fb26f1b55045298edac2ccd2d99}{f}} \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a012a850e4f6231372e95c39aff5d5787}{that}} is only present on the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} It can be transported within the moving \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} by the standard mechanisms of advection and but changes in the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} area can also induce changes in its concentration The \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ac5f0c50a2d71349b887edce57abea84a}{formulation}} of \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} transport equations has been discussed many times in the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ac79d3d8efe3b69d0d73dd502db373caf}{literature}} and the main confusion surrounds how material derivatives are taken Unlike the conventional bulk equations the \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27e9deff4486ed317279151dabf63587}{surface}} does not occupy every point in the so one cannot simply use the standard form of the material derivative Rather than covering the here we shall simply$<$ em $>$ ab the governing equations formulated by \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a27a5a7c1185eb8ef1be6471e61760c76}{Huang}}

summation convention \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_a012a850e4f6231372e95c39aff5d5787}{that}} repeated Roman indices are to be summed over the range from to \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ad1745fb26f1b55045298edac2ccd2d99}{f}} \$n \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ad1745fb26f1b55045298edac2ccd2d99}{f}} and repeated Greek indices are to be summed over the range from to \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ad1745fb26f1b55045298edac2ccd2d99}{f}} \$n \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_ad1745fb26f1b55045298edac2ccd2d99}{f}} We will retain the summation signs for all other such as \mbox{\hyperlink{surface__theory_8txt_af20a0eaa8e1c5ba74c78a8c1b0ac6518}{sums}} over the nodes etc The covariant base vectors of the
